***паршивый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:паршивый.html>парши́вый</a> (7830)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">парша́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paršá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mange</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паршивый.html>парши́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">paršívyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>scabby, mangy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паршивый.html>парши́вая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:овца.html>овца́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стадо.html>ста́до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:портить.html>по́ртит</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">paršívaja ovcá vsjó stádo pórtit</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one black sheep will mar a whole flock</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nasty, rotten, lousy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href class="mention-tr tr Latn">paskúda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">по́скудзь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">паскудьнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paskudĭnŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">poor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = Synchronically derivable from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">па-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pa-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ску́д(ный)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skúd(nyj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-a</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***пасмурный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пасмурный.html>па́смурный</a> (13850)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">па́смурь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pásmurʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасмурный.html>па́смурный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pásmurnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>dull, cloudy, overcast</li>
<li>gloomy, sullen</li></ol>

***паспорт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:паспорт.html>паспорт</a> (1999)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">passaporto</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паспорт.html>па́спорт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pásport</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паспорт.html>па́спорта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паспорт.html>паспорта́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паспорт.html>паспорто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>passport</li>
<li>ID card <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Russia</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>(product) certificate, manual</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In Russia, there are two distinct types of passports: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заграничный.html>заграни́чный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:паспорт.html>па́спорт</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zagraníčnyj pásport</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (i.e. <i>foreign passport</i>) and <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внутренний.html>вну́тренний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:паспорт.html>па́спорт</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vnútrennij pásport</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (i.e. <i>internal or domestic passport</i>). The former is used for traveling abroad and the latter is a standard ID.</li></ul>

***пассаж.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пассаж.html>пасса́ж</a> (16899)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">passage</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пассаж.html>пасса́ж</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">passáž</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пассаж.html>пасса́жа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пассаж.html>пасса́жи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пассаж.html>пасса́жей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>arcade, passage <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">covered passage, usually with shops on both sides</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> passage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>  unexpected turn <i>(of events)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пассаж.html>пасса́ж</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kakoj <b>passáž</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what a thing to happen!; what a turn-up!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***пассажирский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пассажирский.html>пассажи́рский</a> (8262)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пассажир.html>пассажи́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">passažír</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пассажирский.html>пассажи́рский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">passažírskij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> passenger, commuter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пассажирский.html>пассажи́рский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>по́езд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>passažírskij</b> pójezd</i> ― <span class="e-translation">passenger train</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пассажирский.html>пассажи́рский</a></b> самолёт</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>passažírskij</b> samoljót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">passenger plane, airline</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пассия.html>па́ссия</a> (32375)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пассия.html>па́ссия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pássija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пассия.html>па́ссии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пассия.html>па́ссии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пассия.html>па́ссий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>passion, flame (object of passionate love or strong interest)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">паст-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">past-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бище</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-bišče</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***пасти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасти</a> (15961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pastì</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*peh₂-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pastí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to graze, to pasture, to shepherd</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to follow, to tail
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  Андрей Юрьевич <a href = vnd.unilang:курок.html>Курко́в</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andrey_Kurkov" class="extiw" title="w:Andrey Kurkov">Andrey Yuryevich Kurkov</a>),  chapter 54, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>Игра́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отрезанный.html>отре́занный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>палец</a></cite> |  translated as George Bird, transl., <cite>The Case of the General's Thumb</cite>, <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide a date or year)</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:джинсовый.html>джи́нсовых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:костюм.html>костю́мах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удирать.html>удира́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> ки́ева <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́дующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>сме́рти</a> брони́цкого... <a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́х</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасли́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> по́льше <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:граница.html>грани́цы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> герма́нией.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dvóje v džínsovyx kostjúmax udiráli iz Kíjeva na slédujuščij denʹ pósle smérti Broníckovo... Dvóje drugíx <b>paslí</b> ix v Pólʹše do granícy s Germánijej.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The two men in denim suits hopped it from Kiev the day after Bronitsky died. The other two <b>tailed</b> them from Poland to the German frontier.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пастушок.html>пастушо́к</a> (14983)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пастух.html>пасту́х</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastúx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пастушок.html>пастушо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pastušók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пастушок.html>пастушка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пастушок.html>пастушки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пастушок.html>пастушко́в</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пастушо́нок</b>)

***пастырь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пастырь.html>па́стырь</a> (24416)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Uncertain. A borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pastor</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shepherd</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> through a Germanic intermediary or a derivation directly from <i><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасти</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pasti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></i> are both problematic.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Some posit a derivation from a non-attested <i>*пастъ</i> with the same meaning.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пастырь.html>па́стырь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pástyrʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пастырь.html>па́стыря</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пастырь.html>па́стыри</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пастырь.html>па́стырей</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">па́стырский</b>)

***пасть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a> (5493)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pasti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pàsti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pastʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:падать.html>па́дать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> decision<span class="ib-comma">,</span> especially by lot</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall on an option
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ш</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выбор.html>вы́бор</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>па́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Náš výbor <b>pál</b> na pérvyj variánt.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Our choice <b>fell</b> on the first option.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> high register</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall, to die on the battlefield, to be killed in action</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> formal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of historical states, governments</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall, to lose power, to cease to exist, to be toppled</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> formal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of historical cities, castles</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall, to give way under siege
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пройти.html>прошло́</a> ме́ньше <a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>ве́ка</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприступный.html>непристу́пный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>за́мок</a> всё-таки́ <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́рами</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:казацкий.html>каза́цкой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конница.html>ко́нницы</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Prošló ménʹše véka, i nepristúpnyj zámok vsjó-takí <b>pal</b> pod udárami kazáckoj kónnicy.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">After less than a century, even the impenetrable castle <b>fell</b> to the blows of the Cossack cavalry.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stoop, to lower one's morals
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>До</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пени</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:низкий.html>ни́зко</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>па́сть</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пресмыкаться.html>пресмыка́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> тира́ном-захва́тчиком, <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мечтать.html>мечта́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поставить.html>поста́вить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:колено.html>коле́ни</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Do kakój stépeni nádo tak nízko <b>pástʹ</b>, štóby presmykátʹsja pered tiránom-zaxvátčikom, kotóryj mečtájet postávitʹ vesʹ mír na koléni?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">To what extent would one have to <b>stoop</b> so low as to grovel before the tyrant conqueror who wants to put the whole world under his thumb?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>Note that this verb has two past active participle forms: <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:падший.html>па́дший</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pádšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the religious/moral sense, and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>па́вший</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pávšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for all other senses.</li></ul>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Attested since 1731. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pastь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pasti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-tь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pastʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>па́сти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>па́сти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>па́стей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mouth, maw, jaws (of an animal, reptile or fish)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mouth, piehole
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрыть.html>закро́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zakrój <b>pastʹ</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shut up!, shut your piehole!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>throat</li>
<li>wide inlet on a device, structure or construction</li>
<li>trap, snare</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="региональное">рег. (Перм., Новг. Арх., Ленингр., Орл., <a href = vnd.unilang:ворон.html>Ворон</a>., <a href = vnd.unilang:краснодар.html>Краснодар</a>., Волгогр., Пенз.)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасти́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:скот.html>скот</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:птица.html>пти́цу</a>) <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="региональное">рег. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пасший.html>па́сший</a> (5493)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***патетический.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:патетический.html>патети́ческий</a> (26631)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pathét(ique)</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παθητικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pathētikós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:патетический.html>патети́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">patɛtíčeskij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> full of pathos, impassioned, passionate, emotional
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:патетический.html>патети́ческая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>речь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>patɛtíčeskaja</b> rečʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>impassioned</b> speech</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<table style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" width="210" class="morfotable ru">
